\"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udce4 STEP 5: Creating upload service...\"\n\nmkdir -p \"$VV/src/services\"\n\ncat > \"$VV/src/services/uploadService.ts\" << 'UPLOADSERVICE'\n/**\n * Upload Service\n * Handles uploadPdfCatalog(file: File): Promise<UploadResult> {\n    const formData = new FormData();\n    formData.append('file', file);\n    \n    try {\n        console.log('[Upload] Sending PDF to selector);\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        fillingRef.current = true;\n        element.focus();\n        element.classList.add('vv-filling');\n        \n        // Clear and type\n        element.value = '';\n        for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {\n            element.value = text.substring(0, i + 1);\n            \n            // Dispatch events for React\n            element.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));\n            element.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));\n            \n            await new Promise(r => \n        for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(formData)) {\n            if (!value || typeof value !== 'string') continue;\n            \n            const selector = fields[field];\n            if (selector) {\n                await typeIntoField(selector, value);\n                onFill?.(field, value);\n            }\n        }\n    }, [fields, typeIntoField, onFill]);\n    \n    const { }\n    });\n    \n    return null; // This is a logic-only component\n}\n\nexport default VoiceFormFiller;\nVOICEFORMFILLER\n\necho \"  \u2705 Created */\n\nimport React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface PdfUploaderProps {\n    onSuccess?: (data: any) => void;\n    onError?: (error: string) => void;\n    children?: useState(0);\n    \n    const handleUpload = useCallback(async (file: File) => {\n        if (!file) return;\n        \n        setUploading(true);\n        setProgress(10);\n        \n        const fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/upload/pdf', {\n                method: 'POST',\n                body: formData\n            });\n            \n            setProgress(70);\n            \n setProgress(100);\n            \n            console.log('[PdfUploader] Success:', data);\n            onSuccess?.(data);\n            \n        } catch (err: any) {\n            console.error('[PdfUploader] Error:', err);\n            onError?.(err.message || 'Upload failed');\n        } finally {\n            setUploading(false);\n            setTimeout(() => setProgress(0), 1000);\n        }\n    }, [onSuccess, onError]);\n    \n    const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n        const file = e.target.files?.[0];\n        if (file) handleUpload(file);\n    };\n    \n    const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        const file = e.dataTransfer.files?.[0];\n        if (file) handleUpload(file);\n    };\n    \n    return (\n        <div \n            onDrop={handleDrop}\n            onDragOver={e => e.preventDefault()}\n            style={{ position: 'relative' }}\n        >\n            <input\n                type=\"file\"\n                accept=\".pdf\"\n                onChange={handleChange}\n                style={{ display: 'none' }}\n                id=\"pdf-upload-input\"\n            />\n            <label htmlFor=\"pdf-upload-input\" style={{ cursor: 'pointer', display: 'block' }}>\n                {children || (\n                    <div </div>\n                            </>\n                        ) : (\n                            <>\n                                <div style={{ fontSize: '40px', marginBottom: '10px' };\n    \n    const config = statusConfig[state] || statusConfig.idle;\n    \n    const containerStyle: React.CSSProperties = position === 'bottom' ? {\n        position: 'fixed',\n        bottom: \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udd27 STEP 3: Creating VoiceFormFiller component...\\\"\\n\\nmkdir -p \\\"$VV/src/components/voice\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/src/components/voice/VoiceFormFiller.tsx\\\" << 'VOICEFORMFILLER'\\n/**\\n * VoiceFormFiller - Drop-in component that fills form fields from voice\\n * \\n * Usage:\\n *   <VoiceFormFiller \\n *     fields={{ companyName: '#company-input', description: '#desc-input' }}\\n *     onFill={(field, value) => setFormData(prev => ({...prev, [field]: value}))}\\n *   />\\n */\\n\\nimport React, { useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\nimport { useVoice } from '../../hooks/useVoice';\\n\\ninterface VoiceFormFillerProps {\\n    fields: Record<string, string>;  // { fieldName: 'selector' }\\n    context?: string;\\n    onFill?: (field: string, value: string) => void;\\n    onTranscript?: (text: string) => void;\\n    typingSpeed?: number;\\n}\\n\\nexport function VoiceFormFiller({\\n    fields,\\n    context = 'form',\\n    onFill,\\n    onTranscript,\\n    typingSpeed = 25\\n}: VoiceFormFillerProps) {\\n    const fillingRef = useRef(false);\\n    \\n    // Typewriter effect\\n    const typeIntoField = useCallback(async (selector: string, text: string) => {\\n        const element = document.querySelector(selector) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\\n        if (!element) {\\n            console.warn('[VoiceFormFiller] Element not found:', selector);\\n            return;\\n        }\\n        \\n        fillingRef.current = true;\\n        element.focus();\\n        element.classList.add('vv-filling');\\n        \\n        // Clear and type\\n        element.value = '';\\n        for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {\\n            element.value = text.substring(0, i + 1);\\n            \\n            // Dispatch events for React\\n            element.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));\\n            element.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));\\n            \\n            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, typingSpeed));\\n        }\\n        \\n        element.classList.remove('vv-filling');\\n        element.classList.add('vv-filled');\\n        setTimeout(() => element.classList.remove('vv-filled'), 1000);\\n        \\n        fillingRef.current = false;\\n    }, [typingSpeed]);\\n    \\n    // Handle voice response with form data\\n    const handleResponse = useCallback(async (data: any) => {\\n        const formData = data?.formData?.fields;\\n        if (!formData) return;\\n        \\n        console.log('[VoiceFormFiller] Got fields:', formData);\\n        \\n        for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(formData)) {\\n            if (!value || typeof value !== 'string') continue;\\n            \\n            const selector = fields[field];\\n            if (selector) {\\n                await typeIntoField(selector, value);\\n                onFill?.(field, value);\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }, [fields, typeIntoField, onFill]);\\n    \\n    const { transcript, interimTranscript } = useVoice({\\n        context,\\n        onResponse: handleResponse,\\n        onTranscript: (text, isFinal) => {\\n            if (isFinal) onTranscript?.(text);\\n        }\\n    });\\n    \\n    return null; // This is a logic-only component\\n}\\n\\nexport default VoiceFormFiller;\\nVOICEFORMFILLER\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Created \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udce4 STEP 4: Creating PdfUploader component...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/src/components/voice/PdfUploader.tsx\\\" << 'PDFUPLOADER'\\n/**\\n * PdfUploader - Handles PDF   children?: React.ReactNode;\\n}\\n\\nexport function PdfUploader({ onSuccess, onError, children }: PdfUploaderProps) {\\n    const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);\\n    const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\\n    \\n    const handleUpload = useCallback(async (file: File) => {\\n        if (!file) return;\\n        \\n        setUploading(true);\\n        setProgress(10);\\n        \\n        const formData = new FormData();\\n        formData.append('file', file);\\n        \\n        try {\\n            setProgress(30);\\n            \\n            const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/upload/pdf', {\\n                method: 'POST',\\n                body: formData\\n            });\\n            \\n            setProgress(70);\\n            \\n            if (!response.ok) {\\n                throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${response.status}`);\\n            }\\n            \\n            const data = await response.json();\\n            setProgress(100);\\n            \\n            console.log('[PdfUploader] Success:', data);\\n            onSuccess?.(data);\\n            \\n        } catch (err: any) {\\n            console.error('[PdfUploader] Error:', err);\\n            onError?.(err.message || 'Upload failed');\\n        } finally {\\n            setUploading(false);\\n            setTimeout(() => setProgress(0), 1000);\\n        }\\n    }, [onSuccess, onError]);\\n    \\n    const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\\n        const file = e.target.files?.[0];\\n        if (file) handleUpload(file);\\n    };\\n    \\n    const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\\n        e.preventDefault();\\n        const file = e.dataTransfer.files?.[0];\\n        if (file) handleUpload(file);\\n    };\\n    \\n    return (\\n        <div \\n            onDrop={handleDrop}\\n            onDragOver={e => e.preventDefault()}\\n            style={{ position: 'relative' }}\\n        >\\n            <input\\n                type=\\\"file\\\"\\n                accept=\\\".pdf\\\"\\n                onChange={handleChange}\\n                style={{ display: 'none' }}\\n                id=\\\"pdf-upload-input\\\"\\n            />\\n            <label htmlFor=\\\"pdf-upload-input\\\" style={{ cursor: 'pointer', display: 'block' }}>\\n                {children || (\\n                    <div style={{\\n                        border: '2px dashed #4a5568',\\n                        borderRadius: '12px',\\n                        padding: '40px',\\n                        textAlign: 'center',\\n                        background: uploading ? 'rgba(6, 182, 212, 0.1)' : 'transparent'\\n                    }}>\\n                        {uploading ? (\\n                            <>\\n                                <div style={{ fontSize: '24px', marginBottom: '10px' }}>\\ud83d\\udce4</div>\\n                                <div>Uploading... {progress}%</div>\\n                                <div style={{\\n                                    height: '4px',\\n                                    background: '#1a202c',\\n                                    borderRadius: '2px',\\n                                    marginTop: '10px',\\n                                    overflow: 'hidden'\\n                                }}>\\n                                    <div style={{\\n                                        width: `${progress}%`,\\n                                        height: '100%',\\n                                        background: 'linear-gradient(90deg, #06b6d4, #8b5cf6)',\\n                                        transition: 'width 0.3s'\\n                                    }} />\\n                                </div>\\n                            </>\\n                        ) : (\\n                            <>\\n                                <div style={{ fontSize: '40px', marginBottom: '10px' }}>\\ud83d\\udcc4</div>\\n                                <div>Click or drag PDF to upload</div>\\n                            </>\\n                        )}\\n                    </div>\\n                )}\\n            </label>\\n        </div>\\n    );\\n}\\n\\nexport default PdfUploader;\\nPDFUPLOADER\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Created \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83c\\udf9b\\ufe0f STEP 5: Creating AgenticBarWithFill component...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/src/components/voice/AgenticBarWithFill.tsx\\\" << 'AGENTICBARFILL'\\n/**\\n *          await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 25));\\n        }\\n        \\n        element.classList.remove('vv-filling');\\n        element.classList.add('vv-filled');\\n        setTimeout(() => {config.icon} {state.toUpperCase()}\\n                        </span>\\n                    </div>\\n                    <span style={{\\n                        fontSize: '11px',\\n                        padding: '2px 8px',\\n                        borderRadius: '10px',\\n                        background: 'rgba(6, 182, 212, 0.2)',\\n                        color: '#06b6d4'\\n Filling\\n\\n## In VendorFlow.tsx (Business Profile Step):\\n\\n```tsx\\nimport { AgenticBarWithFill } from '@/components/voice';\\n\\nfunction BusinessProfileStep({ formData, setFormData }) {\\n Profile</h2>\\n            \\n            {/* Add IDs to your inputs */}\\n            <input \\n                id=\\\"company-name-input\\\"\\n                value={formData.companyName}\\n                onChange={e => setFormData(prev => ({...prev, companyName: e.target.value}))}\\n                placeholder=\\\"Company Name\\\"\\n            />\\n            \\n            <textarea\\n                id=\\\"company-description\\\"\\n                value={formData.description}\\n                onChange={e => setFormData(prev => ({...prev, description: e.target.value}))}\\n
